Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	"If you feel the wire and between your two fingers there is the tissue or sphincter or flesh where it is about to pierce, then there is nothing but hope and expectation, through the administration of one of these three methods:"
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	"either you cauterize it as we have said, or cut it all the way through, or if you push it there with wires and treat it as before;"
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	"and do not go too deep that you cut the tissue that holds the anus in place, and let evacuations come out without voluntary effort;"
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then the treatment, as we have said
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	perhaps it will heal on its own, or you may remove that covering and clean it after it has grown close to the base, using a probe or some other pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then uncover the cloth bandage that is on the wound as much as you can
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then examine how to restore the wound and keep the fistula in its position behind the fundament; this will be easier for the patient
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes fistulas occur in this manner: when you insert the tent into the fistula and it is located on the side of the fundament near the skin above
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	if take a pierced tube at its head according to this shape
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And I twist one thread into two, and insert the tube along with all the thread into the fistula until it reaches the top
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it passes through the margin of the fundament inward, then remove the thread from that opening so that you insert your finger into the fundament
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	and tie the head of the thread, and bring the two ends together, and tie them to each other tightly, leaving it on for one or two days
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and tighten it sometimes until the threads cut through those tissues that are between them and open
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then heal the wound until it is healed and clean
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open on its own, then make an opening for it in all ways that you can, if it is not too deep
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not necessary to break open a fistula that is too deep, and then heal it as we have said until it is clean
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the pointed bistoury used to make an opening for the fistula is most like one part and cutting
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and the other part not, because we do not cut that which we should not cut, as you can see here
des emorroydes	hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are of two kinds: some are inside the fundament, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and sometimes there is blood on the surface
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	and some have one or many, and they are behind the fundament and at the head of the fundament; but those that are behind have little moisture
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	and on their surface there is sometimes a little clear water or a little blood, and they are the color of flesh
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the cure for those who have hemorrhoids inside the fundament is that you tell the patient to strain while going to the privy until the fundament protrudes and the veins appear
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	then act quickly, and pinch it with forceps or hold it with your fingernail, then cut it at its root
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the fingers cannot hold them because of their moisture, then take them with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of leather
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And pull out both [of your arms], then cut them, and powder with some warm powders that are in place of cautery
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other treatments until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the foundation cannot come out, then apply a clister of biting and harsh medicine to wash what is in the foundation so that it can come out clearly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patient takes care [of themselves], and if the threads are outside of the foundation, then the treatment is easy
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you grasp them with your fingernail or forceps and cut them off, then treat them as we have said until they are healed, and so that there is fear of cutting with a knife
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	It is necessary that you arrange the stitching in this manner: take one twisted thread and insert it into a needle, then draw the thread upwards and pierce the needle on the other side, and wrap the two ends of the thread under the needle
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and let it be thick; and tie the thread tightly, then knot the thread, and remove the needle, and do this with all the others, and leave one for correcting any excess of blood
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place on top of the foundation one damp cloth moistened in rose oil or in wax, and place it on the foundation, and tell the patient to rest
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let him alone until they fall out, and when they have fallen out, treat them with ointment and other treatments until they are healed
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	Regarding the drying of phlegm in the foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is a drying of phlegm in the intestines, either due to constriction of nature or when the disease is old and medicines are ineffective
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you remove with the point of a spoon or your fingernail the outer skin which does not let it become moist;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then perform the treatment until it is solid as it ought to be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot hold fast, then resume the scraping more forcefully than before until it becomes smooth and is scraped clean;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then perform the treatment until it is healed.
dou fremit	trembles
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	An ant is a tiny creature that moves around inside the body and is very difficult to detect;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	"And sometimes cold seizes him, and he feels it like death's trembling, spreading throughout his body, but more so in the hands than elsewhere."
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	"And the treatment is to take a goose feather quill or a strong swan feather and place it on the trembling [joint] until the circle enclosing the trembling is complete;"
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	"then rotate your hand around the quill so that you grasp all around the trembling [joint], and push it in deeply, and crush the trembling at its root."
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	"And if you see, do this with a reed or iron rod in accordance with this form, and let it be thin below and tapering above:"
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	"Do not pierce it, so that you can hold the two [joints] together and press them tightly. And if you see fit, cauterize the trembling as is described in the chapter on cautery."
de la forme dou clistere	"of the form of the clyster"
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	"Sometimes a silver or steel clyster is made, sometimes one of molten brass or iron; and sometimes they are made of these small or large instruments, according to their size."
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	"Those that are used in the treatment of children and those who are weak and painful are small."
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	"The form of the small and large clyster is as follows: wide where the belly is tied in this manner:"
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	"And there should be an opening where the belly is tied, as you see here, and the feces should be pierced inside; and it should have two holes on one side and one hole on the other;"
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	"And let the belly where one puts the medicines be made of an animal bladder or parchment, and pierced all around with small holes,"
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	"and let there be a drop of spice between each hole, then insert one strong thread of coarse yarn twisted into ten or fifteen loops around it, and tie the belly like a goat's;"
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	"And when the medicine is inside, first tie it to the instrument beforehand with a strong thread, then perform the clyster; and this is the form of the circle:"
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	"And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and grease the end of the clyster with oil or egg yolk, or something similar, then insert it gently;"
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	"Then the minister squeezes with both hands together until it is all expelled, then remove the clyster and have the patient raise their legs towards the bed;"
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	"and if the medicine wants to come out, let it be retained as much as possible; and if he lies all night, it is more helpful."
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if you perform a clyster in the case of diarrhea of the belly, and the medicine rushes out quickly, then recommence it until it is retained."
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	"And if the hemorrhoids are in the fundament or fistulous ulcer, let the clyster be as small as for one child;"
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	"And this is the form of the thin clyster when the skin is stretched taut:"
des plaies	"wounds"
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	"We have already spoken in the division about the treatment of wounds; now we will tell you about the treatments for hands and medicines according to their completion."
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	"I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and of what they are made."
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	"The things by which wounds are made are: stones thrown from a sling, cuts from swords and daggers or spears or clubs or similar weapons;"
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	"or those that are made according to the places on the body, such as wounds that fall on the neck, or head, or face, or belly, or liver, and similar members;"
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	"And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and will begin with simple head wounds, for the memory will come in its chapter."
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	"I say that when a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, one should take care if it was caused by a stone or something similar, and if the skin is entirely torn and the wound is large,"
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	"and if it is a hot fistulous ulcer, then clean it promptly with cold water especially if there is little blood coming from the wound, and let the washing be on the opposite side of the wounded part;"
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	"And keep the patient from eating too much meat and wine."
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	"And if he does not want to clean it, then let his food be reduced, and let him drink neither wine nor eat meat;"
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	"and put on the wound, if a hot fistulous ulcer comes, cotton moistened in rose oil alone, or in wine that is styptic;"
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	"And if there is no hot fistulous ulcer, then put on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood, and not moved by the air, powder that I will tell you about later;"
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if the air has moved it, then put on some ointments until it is clean."
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	"And if the wound is large, like a sword cut or similar ones, and its lips cannot be brought together by tying, then bring them together with stitches, as I will tell you about in the treatment of abdominal wounds, regarding stitching."
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	"If the wound is exposed to the bone and hanging, and only held by a little bit of skin, then cut it off; then treat the wound with medicines, and restore hard flesh in place of skin,"
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	"and command the patient to eat large quantities of meat, such as testicles and cooked wheat, also poultry and similar things."
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	"And if you find rottenness in the skin and it has not reached the bone, then cut off all the rotting flesh and clean it out, then treat it;"
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	"And if there is an artery or vein in the wound that is bare and cannot be stopped by medicines, then find the artery, and if you find it dislocated, tie it with a thread;"
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	"And if this does not help, then cauterize it."
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	"And if these wounds are small and simple, their treatment is easy; and this is what you should do: put in this powder that seals before the air moves it."
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	"The manner of making the powder is: take incense in one part; dragon's blood two parts; quicklime three parts, and grind it finely;"
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	"and fill the wound and press it firmly until it is well sealed and joined with all its blood;"
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	"And then bind it well and let it remain without removing the dressing until it is healed, for one does not remove the medicine until it is healed."
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	"Sometimes they do this with quicklime alone, when they do not have incense or dragon's blood, but the air has not moved the wound."
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	"And if the air has moved the wound, especially in summer, do not put this powder on it at all;"
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	"but put on some digested ointments or poultices made from barley flour with water and honey until it softens;"
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	"then treat it with other treatments until it is healed."
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	"And if bone fragments come with the wound and it is small, then extract them with fine forceps;"
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	"and I will tell you about head fractures later."
de la plaie dou col	"Regarding wounds on the neck:"
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	"If a wound comes to the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between it and one on the head, except that if the nerve of the neck or an artery is cut."
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerves, there is no other remedy but to leave them alone and not apply anything constricting, for it harms the nerves and causes them to retreat.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	Do not apply anything cold to the wound, for nerve tissue is cold, and its extension is connected to the brain, which is the highest organ.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	But if any medication is used, it should be warm, such as warm water mixed with rose oil and cooked also in soft water
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other medicaments prepared in this manner, and moist applications.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, it should be stitched and bound with bandages until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	If wounds are deep and filled with bowels, then pierce them lower down.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is cut and blood is flowing profusely, expose it, ligate it, and cauterize it if necessary
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the windpipe or the heart is cut, but the vessels are preserved through which life goes
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	then stitch up the heart against the spine of the neck, and do not touch the throat, but place it back in its natural position
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then bind it firmly, leave it for a few days, and then treat it with drying ointments until it heals
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	If the wound has made an impression on the bone, scrape it out.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	And if there are bone fragments, remove all those you can reach with forceps, and leave those that you cannot have until the wound suppurates
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and evacuate and ligate the outlet
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, powder it with the powder that I have mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	If there are bones and fistulas in the wound, treat it as I have said in its chapter
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	Chapter on wounds made by a spear or dagger
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a wound made by a spear or dagger and the wound is deep, observe if wind passes through it when the patient breathes. Know then that the wound is mortal
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	And if it is not deep but fresh with all its blood, do not put powder on it at first nor bind it so that the blood does not flow out deeply
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and let it return to the heart and kill the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply an attractive ointment, and cover it twice a day
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you have no ointment, then place some wool cotton in the wound to suck out the moisture
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and make the patient lie on the affected area for 3 or 4 days, or longer
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if no spasm comes, nor trembling of the heart, nor twitching of the nerves
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see signs of recovery, know that the wound is healed
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Therefore treat it with plasters and other remedies until it heals
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot heal nor close up, then know that there is a fistula present, and treat it accordingly
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a cut made by a sword or knife, whether simple or deep or on the back, treat it as one would for wounds in front of the body
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it is large, stitch it up; and if it is small, powder it; and if it has entered the bone or has cut off pieces of flesh, remove the wound, and treat them separately if they are severed
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not severed, let the wound suppurate until the extraneous matter is expelled
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds on other members, judge them as we have said
dou derrompement dou ventre	on bursting of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	Bursting of the belly may be great or medium or small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	"Sometimes, due to a large wound, an intestine or part of it protrudes; therefore..."
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	"And stitching is more painful, and sometimes a small wound hurts worse than a large one,"
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	"because it's easier to gently push the intestines back in place if they haven't been heated up."
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	"For the intestines swell quickly when cold and thus are harder to gently put back in place,"
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	"And therefore it is better to move the smaller wound, because one can more easily move the intestine back into its place than others that are deeper."
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	"And know that there are four ways to treat a burst abdomen:"
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	"The two common sutures happen during abdominal surgery,"
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	"and the suture of other wounds on the body and two other specific sutures are common to other wounds;"
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	"However, they are more appropriate with abdominal surgery, and I will explain each one and clarify them."
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	"I say that when the wound is small and nothing has spilled out of the intestines,"
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	"and if there's little else to do besides putting it back in place, one should choose one of these two methods:"
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	"or because the wound is small, as we have said,"
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	"or because the intestines are swollen due to cold."
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	"And when it's cold, warm it up this way:"
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	"Wet one sponge or cloth with hot water alone,"
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	"or boil it in water with vinegar and saffron,"
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	"And warm the intestines until the swelling is gone;"
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	"And afterwards apply this soothing remedy, and it's best if done with a warm hand for unraveling."
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	"And when you see the swelling leaving, then mix the intestines with hot water or sweet wine that has been cooked with spices,"
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	"because this way it's easier to put them back in place;"
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	"And if they can't fit back in, then make a small incision with the instrument used to cut hemorrhoids;"
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	"And the first method is best when the wound is made by a knife,"
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	"That no one should make without good reason."
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	"And this is the instrument to cut it open:"
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	"So cut inside the curve and not outside, and here you see its shape:"
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	"And when the wound is enlarged and intestines have spilled out,"
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	"then put them back gently according to their natural shape in their proper place;"
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	"If you're able to do so, for that's best."
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	"When the wound is large and it's below the belly button,"
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	"You must have the patient lie on their back like this:"
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	"And lift their legs higher than their head;"
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	"And if it's below the belly button,"
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	If you place the head and chest higher than the parts below
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and likewise if the intestine is ruptured in one of the two sections
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	then ensure that the injured part is higher than the other
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus one must arrange what I say in both large and moderate wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	In small wounds, apply whatever you have
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then take a compassionate assistant who will remove all the rupture with his hand
et assemble les levres;	and bring the lips together
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common way of suturing
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	It is necessary to take one needle or several according to the quantity of the width of the wound
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave two spaces from the beginning of the wound and insert a needle with a good strong thread
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce both sides of the skin with both sides of the silk
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is underneath the skin within, until you have pierced all that part
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and bring together the two ends of the silk with four knots together
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then tighten a doubled thread around the needle on both sides
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then bring together both edges of the wound evenly
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave two spaces and insert another needle
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie off the thread just as you did with the first needle
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue doing this according to how many needles you need
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	Until all the wound is restricted;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and let the needles be medium-sized, between fine and coarse
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	for fine needles cut all the flesh and those too large cannot enter well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	Therefore they must be medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it is not necessary to push the needles too deep into the flesh and skin
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	lest they cut and open the wound before the suture.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	Then cut off the tips of the needles so that they do not prick the patient while sleeping
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and put cloths or bandages on the tips of the needles to hold them better
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them there until the wound is healed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	And this method of suturing with needles is more suitable for small wounds
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it takes only one needle or two
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second suture is common
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and it consists in bringing together the two edges of the skin and the two edges of the flesh with one needle and strong medium-sized thread;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	And when you have pierced all these edges together
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then turn the needle back towards where you started, in the way one sews cloth
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and leave a space between each stitch the thickness of a small finger;
ceste costure sevent li home,	This suture is used by men
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	I once sewed a wound in the belly of a man
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	who was stabbed with a knife
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than a palm's length long
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	And there were about two palms' worth of intestines sticking out
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	And the wound was in his belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	"I then reset the intestines after he had been ill for twenty-four hours."
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	"And the wound was healed up to fifteen days, and I treated it, and it was well."
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	"And the physicians judged that he would die, but it was a miracle."
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	"and I did not treat him with ointment because I was in one place where there was none to be found nor any medicine."
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	"and I placed old cotton on the wound twice a day and washed it with honey water until it was healed."
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	"I will now tell you the two proper methods of sewing:"
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	"Take the needle and thrust it from the outer part to the inner."
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	"When the needle has pierced directly through the heart, then lay its head down on the scabbard or the place where you have inserted the needle,"
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	"and make it pierce from the inner part to the outer."
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	"And the meaning of this sewing is that you should stitch in the same way as a tanner prepares hides,"
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	"and that you leave the needle once on one side and take it up again on the other, until the stitching is complete."
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	"The second method of sewing, which Galen describes as proper,"
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	"is when one brings together the two parts naturally and assembles them."
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	"And they apply one end of the needle to the other in this way:"
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	"Stick a needle into the nearby skin and make it pierce only that spot,"
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	"And leave the two ends of the needle."
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	"Then turn the needle and make it pierce from the outer part to the inner,"
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	"And leave the two ends of the needle."
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	"Then make both ends pierce from the outer part to the inner in two other nearby places that are on the other side,"
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	"And this is the mother and most common method of sewing."
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	"Galen spoke these words, and some testify to them,"
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	"That one should sew the belly with two needles, each having thread on it,"
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	"And one must thrust in one needle from one side and the other from the other, like those who sew hides."
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	"And know that when theulture is inside the belly,"
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	"the stitching will be more tense than in other places of the belly."
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	"The judgment on the wound is such as for other wounds,"
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	"And it is that when you find the wound fresh with all its blood before the art has moved it,"
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	"then put back the intestines and the skin; then sprinkle powder around the wound."
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	"And if the art has moved it, then apply some ointment that is nearby until the wound heals."
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	"And cut the thread and sew up the needles and the skin,"
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	"then treat the wound as for others until it is healed."
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	"And if you have no medications, then immediately when it begins to heal put on old cotton,"
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	"and move it twice a day until it is healed."
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	"For in many situations where wounds are simple you have no need of any other medication,"
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	"And if you doubt that the wound does not communicate with the principal members,"
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	"then it is necessary for you to wet light linen in warm oil of roses or rose oil,"
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	"And place it around the angles and under the armpits;"
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	"And if there is pain or putrefaction in the belly, which happens very often,"
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	"then administer warm black wine enemas, and especially if the putrefaction reaches the intestines;"
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	"And pierce it internally, and know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small one."
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	"The intestine called 'jejunum' cannot be healed when it is wounded,"
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	And it is due to the thickness of the veins there,
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the intestine jumps out of the wound, push it back in just like the intestines, while it is still fresh.
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it is old and has turned green or black, then you must tie the place that is black so that blood does not flow from there.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	For there are veins and arteries.
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	Then cut what is between the ligature
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and place the two stitches hanging down from the part below the wound until far enough to help draw out the intestine when it falls and the wound opens.
de la routure dou boueil	of the wound's opening
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestine is removed and the wound is small
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	it can be restored in some cases
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	for I have seen a man wounded in the belly by a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it turned into an abscess and became a fistula through which the digestion and wind escaped
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated him as best I could, and did not cease to care for him until he was completely healed with sound flesh.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw him healed, I doubted that the sick man might have some ailment in his belly
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and there was no illness, but he remained in good condition, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And some surgeons said that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it should be tied in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	Take catgut with large threads, then gather together the edges of the wound
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the catgut has opened its mouth, place it on both lips
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	so that its mouth may stretch open;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	then cut off its head so that it cannot untie itself
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	and then place another catgut afterward in the same manner as before until the wound is completely closed;
et cout la plaie.	And stitch up the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	Those who practice this method find it useful for wounds in the intestine and cause no harm to the patient
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and one can tie the intestine with a fine thread cut from the intestine of an animal.
en teil maniere:	In this manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	Take the head of this gut, let it be very skinned
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie it to the head of this thread, one thread of fine twisted linen,
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Then insert the thread into the needle, and with it sew the intestine, and repair it at the rupture.
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this method of sewing is only appropriate according to the path of trust and hope
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the large intestines, then there is nothing that can cure it except subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of fistula wherever it may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that every wound or boil, when it becomes chronic, is universally called a "fistula",
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	especially when it is deep and curves inward.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And fistula is according to its true nature a hard and white knot or lump, where there is no pain felt
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it is also deep like the quill of a bird
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	and sometimes clear and shallow, other times thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes small, other times quite large;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	and as I have spoken of in the section on wounds, any wound that is not healed and there is no flesh
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	is only caused by one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	namely, by the smallness of blood or flesh;
ou por sa malice;	or due to its wickedness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard flesh inside and on the lips that prevents new flesh from forming
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or if it is too deep;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or if the location is poor and the material is of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or if the medicine used in treatment is not good;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the corruption is in a manner of pestilence.
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or because the property in the region is slow in digestion and healing is delayed by nature.
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or if there are veins or bones exposed:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	And I have already shown all of these causes, signs, and cures with medicines in the relevant section.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	But now I must tell you about the treatment of fistula that is performed by manual labor.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistula can occur in all parts of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	for there are fistulas that come from large veins and arteries and nerves;
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or from the spine, intestines, bladder or any of the ribs;
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or from the spinal cord in the back, or at any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and some that affect the main property of the member itself and similar locations.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all fistulas that are of this kind have difficult healing, with only labor and skill being able to help;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	but if there is any fistula that does not come from the places I mentioned, you can be confident about its treatment;
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	"And you recognize it, so take a tent of tin or iron if the fistula is straight; thus seek it."
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	"And if the fistula is curved, search for it with a subtle tent made of lead."
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	Because the lead bends and moves around the tortuousness
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	And if the fistula is large and perforated, and you cannot tightly encircle it with your hands
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	If you can pass a catheter through one of the openings
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	because moisture comes out from one opening to another, and cleanses it
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then search for bleeding as much as you can, so that you know if there is bone or nerve inside, and how deep it goes
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient carefully about the pain they feel when you press your hand down, and where they feel it
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	And once you know exactly where the dislocation is located, and whether it is far from a joint, nerve, artery or vein
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in any of the places I mentioned, then reduce the dislocation according to what I have told you
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and remove the fractured bone and rotten cartilage that are inside
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	Then treat it until it is healed
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	And if the fistula is very deep in a straight line, you must cut down deeply, as far as possible
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	then place moistened gauze sponges in hot water and insert them up to the head of the fistula
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the hot water dissolves the remaining excess tissue at the bottom
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then apply clean bandages until the wound is healed
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	And if it does not heal with this treatment, then cauterize it as we have said
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if the bone is damaged by the fistula, remove it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If veins or nerves do not interfere with the main limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	"And if the bone is exposed, and there is corruption and blackness, then cleanse until all corruption has been removed"
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	"Then treat with hot poultice until it is healed";
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	"And if he is not healed, and returns as before."
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	"Know that you have not yet reached your goal:"
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	"So search until you find the bottom,"
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	"And remove all corruption, then reset it in place;"
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	"And if he is thus healed, that's good."
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	"If not, know that the corruption goes too deep for you to reach it;"
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	"So there is nothing else to do but leave it to nature."
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	"And if there is even the slightest bone corrupted, you can extract it with forceps,"
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	"If extracted by one of these instruments,"
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	"And if there are many bones, grind them all to dust and leave none intact;"
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	"And if the moistures resist you, and there is no mistake nor fear,"
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	"So cut through flesh and moisture, and expose the bones."
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	"And if you cannot remove them within an hour, place something irritating to corruption on the wound,"
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	"and leave it there until the flesh around the bones has rotted away;"
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	"And then the bones will come out more easily."
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	"And if it is a large bone, such as from the leg or thigh,"
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	"So remove only the corruption until all blackness has been removed;"
puis restoure la plaie;	"then close the wound;"
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	"And if there is much corrupted flesh coming right up to the bone,"
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	If it must be, then it should be covered entirely up to corruption, and then cured until it is solid.
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	and I will tell you about a fistula that happened in one leg of a man
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	so that you may take an example and help with your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	There was a young man around 30 years old who had pain in his leg due to a cause that came from inside the body
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	such that matter came into the leg, and there was a large swelling, but no apparent reason for it to open.
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	but the doctors foolishly operated on it so much that the swelling opened
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	and they cut out a lot of matter, and then it became a fistula with many holes that discharged bowels and moisture from the body
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	and for two years many doctors attempted to treat it, but none were skilled in this art of hands
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	until I was called and saw his leg and the medications that they were using to treat it
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	and what came out of the holes was very foul.
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	The youth's body became red, and had a yellowish hue.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I placed a plug in one of the holes and then searched for all the other holes
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	and found that some came from within others on all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os,	I then hurried and cut into one of the holes until I discovered a part of the bone,
et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	"I found [the bone] corrupted and perforated, with corruption reaching down to the inner bone."
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	"I saw that which appeared to me of the corrupted bone, and thought there was no other corruption besides what I had removed."
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	"And began to dress the wound with caustic medicine for a long time, but it could not heal."
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant,	"Then I resumed, and discovered the bone just as before,"
et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	"And found that the corruption had spread to the bone; I cut it out, and then proceeded to heal the place."
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	"But no sooner had I cut around about a palm's breadth of bone, than the whole was gangrened,"
puis le restourai de medicines; et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment,	"Then I dressed it with medicine again, and it healed quickly."
et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir,	"But there was no need to resume the operation except for the weakness of the patient, who could not bear it,"
et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	"and because of the fear of death that I had for him."
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	"For although he often bled profusely, he was entirely healed,"
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	"And in place of the bone there grew hard flesh, and he was in good condition and had no harm or discomfort at all, neither then nor afterwards."
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	"And if any bone is broken anywhere in the body, it should be treated thus:"
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	"Take one lien, and tie it tightly to the head of the exposed bone,"
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	"And command some to extend it upwards;"
et met .i. autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os,	"and put on another linen band, larger than the first, and tie it above the flesh over the bone,"
et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz,	"And stretch out the head so that you can pull away the decayed flesh underneath,"
et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	"And uncover the flesh over where you see it, lest the wound blacken the flesh."
et met .i. tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	"And place one hot ember or a heated stone under the bone to cauterize the rotting flesh.";
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	"And it is necessary to be as visible and palpable as possible in seeing and feeling the corruption, and also to be repeated again."
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie,	"If the bone is corrupted, and does not appear, and the corruption is in the middle or in one part,"
si descuevre la char toute; puis met .i. tison desoz,	"then uncover all of the flesh; then place a brand underneath,"
et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption .i. poc, si com nos avons dit;	"And then draw the corruption from one part to another with tweezers that are as long as the corruption itself, as we have said;"
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	"If the corruption is in the joint, cut off the corrupted joint and draw out the bone that contains it from the other side."
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des .ij. jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	"And if the corruption is in the continuity of two joints, there is no other remedy than to cut it off."
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose,	"But if the corruption is in the palm of the hand or foot, then it is very serious."
mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	"Nevertheless, you must inquire about this corruption and how it appears to you;"
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	"And cleanse it in all ways that you can, but do not let the veins or nerves oppose you."
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous,	"Know that there are many types of saws and forceps for cutting these bones, according to their arrangement and appearance."
et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	"And also according to their thickness, thinness, length, shortness, and hardness;"
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	"Therefore, it is necessary to equip each type of work with its appropriate instrument."
et saiches que l’uevre te moustrera l’estrument dont tu avras mestier, selonc la conissance de cest art,	"And know that the work will show you which instrument you will need according to your knowledge of this art;"
et le tesmoignaige des manieres des maladies;	"and also based on the testimony of the various diseases."
si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	"So think about which instrument you need according to what is appropriate for the situation."
dou feu	Fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	"The flesh decays either because of an internal cause or because of a cause from outside;"
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie,	"And when you have treated that corruption with remedies, but they do not help,"
si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient,	"then it is necessary to cut off that member up to the place where the corruption comes from."
si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	"So that the patient escapes death through this, or through the loss of the member, which is a lesser evil;"
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu,	"And the sign is that the member becomes black, as if it had been burned by fire."
et porrist aprés la noiror, puis va celle corrosions de membre em membre,	"After the blackness comes, then this corruption spreads from member to member;"
et prent par tout le cors; si te haste dou coper,	"And then it spreads throughout the body; so hurry up and cut it off,"
et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans,	"If it is due to the sting of venomous beasts such as sea scorptions, vipers, and similar creatures;"
se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	"If the corruption is at the top of the thigh, cut it off so that it does not spread down to the hand."
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	"And if it reaches the hand, then cut it off at the joint so that the corruption does not reach the arm;"
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute; et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors,	"And if it reaches the arm, then cut it off at the elbow. And if it passes the elbow, then death is certain."
et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	"and there are no remedies outside of those that can increase its power in sufficient quantity;"
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet: s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	"And likewise, when corruption comes to the foot: if it reaches the first joint, cut it off after the second joint;"
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	"And if it reaches the foot, then cut off the entire foot;"
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	"And if it spreads up to the leg, cut it off at the knee joint;"
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	"And if it goes above the knee, then there is no other option but to let the patient die."
et li maniere dou coper ou dou soier le membre si est que tu le lie desus et desoz,	"And the way to cut off or cauterize a member is to tie it above and below;"
et estende uns menistres l’un des liiens aval, et uns autres ministres l’autre liien amont,	"And have some helpers hold one of the ties downwards, and others pull the other tie upwards;"
et tu dessevre la char qui est entre les .ij. liiens a .i. spatumile large, tant que li os soit descovers;	"and you cut through the flesh that is between the two ties with a broad-bladed scalpel until the bone is exposed;"
puis le cope ou soie, et met de chescune part .i. drapeil de lin, si que li soie ne touche le leu sain,	"then cut it off or cauterize it, and place a linen cloth on each side so that the cautery does not touch the healthy area;"
et viegne au malaide autre lesion et aposteme chaus.	"And then bring the patient another wound and poultice."
Et se decorremens de sanc vient quant tu oevres, si cauterize le leu hastanment,	"If bleeding occurs while you are operating, quickly cauterize the area;"
ou tu met sus aucunes poudres restraignans; puis revien a ta medicine tant qu’elle soit acomplie,	"or apply some restrictive powders. Then return to your treatment until it is complete."
puis lie le membre navreit d’un liien covenauble, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	"Then bind the wounded member with a suitable bandage and treat it until it heals;"
et je te conterai k’il avint a .i. home en som piet:	"And I will tell you what happened to one man regarding his foot:"
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu,	"He had blackness that seemed like it had been burned by fire;"
et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	"And this corruption first appeared on the top of his foot and then spread throughout the entire foot;"
et quant li hons vit la corrosion, si se hasta de coper le piet, et fut sanez;	"But when the man saw the corruption, he hurried to cut off his foot, and it healed;"
et lonc tens aprés li revint li corrosion ou doi de la main, et il vint a moi,	"and some time later, the corruption reappeared on top of his hand, and he came to me;"
et je li mis sus choses repercussives aprés la mundification dou cors, et ne pot cesser li corrosions;	"I applied caustic substances to him after cleaning his body, but the corruption could not be stopped;"
et il vot que je li copasse la main, et je ne vou, que je avoie esperance de repercuter la matiere;	"He wanted me to cut off his hand, but I refused because I had hope that we could stop the spread of the corruption;"
et doutai ausi que se je tailloie sa main, qu’il ne morist,	"I also feared that if I cut off his hand, he would die;"
car li vertus de l’ome estoit foible; et il se despera toz, et revint en sa terre,	"because the man was weak in power. And he became completely discouraged and returned home."
et se hasta de coper sa main, et fut sanez;	"He hurried to cut off his hand, and it healed;"
et je n’ai ceu conteit fuers que por ceu c’on faice autreteil, s’on en a mestier.	"And I tell you this story only so that others may learn from it if they are ever in need."
Aucune fois vient aposteme en leu charnut, et demore si longement qu’il fait grant assemblee de bowe;	"Sometimes an abscess forms on the skin and stays there for such a long time that it becomes very large;"
et puis ront et perce, et en saut li bowe, et demoure li leus vuis, ausi com uns vasselz;	"And then it hardens, bursts open, and when the boil jumps, the area remains empty like an empty vessel;"
et li cuir qui est desus est ausi subtilz com .i. drapelz deliiez,	"The skin that is on top of it becomes as thin as a delicate veil;"
et ne corront mie jusc’a l’os, ne jusc’au nerf, et telz maladie si est apelee «sain»,	"And such illnesses are called 'clean' because they do not go down to the bone or nerve."
et n’est mie apelee «fistule»;	"This is not called a fistula;"
mais s’elle est si alongie qu’elle viegne jusc’a l’os em parfont, si est apelee «fistule»;	"But if it stretches out so much that it reaches the bone and goes deep, then it is called 'fistula';"
et li cuire si est que tu cope celui cuir tout entor, et meismement quant il est subtilz, ausi com uns drapelz;	"And the skin should be cut all around, especially when it is thin like a veil;"
et ne s’aert mie por sa corruption.	"But do not fear its corruption."
Et se tu as fiance que li cuirs s’aerde, et li corruption n’est mie en parfont,	"And if you think that the skin will scar and that the corruption is not deep,"
et li cuir est espés de char, si le cure de clistere ensi:	"and the skin is thick with flesh, then treat it as follows:"
regarde se li seins est grans, et li bowe qui en ist est de puant odor,	"Look to see if the boil is large and whether it smells foul;"
adonques le clisterize de medicine egiptiaine qui est ensi faite:	"Then apply an Egyptian poultice made as follows:"
prenez aisil, et oile, et litargire, igalment, et metez cuire en .i. vassel au feu,	"Take equal parts of onion, oil, and lead filings, place them in a vessel over the fire;"
tant que li medicine soit rouge, et deviegne ausi espesse com miel;	"and cook it until the poultice becomes red and as thick as honey;"
et puis pren de ceu selonc ta necessiteit, et le font en aigue et en miel,	"Then take some of this according to your need, mix it with warm water and honey,"
et en clisterize lou sein, et estraint le pertus;	"And apply the poultice to the boil, and cover the opening tightly;"
et laisse la medicine ens par .ij. houres, puis l’estrai en espreignant;	"Let it remain there for two hours, then remove it by squeezing;"
fai ce mout de fois, tant que li seins soit mondefiiez, et soit ostee li puor;	"Do this repeatedly until the boil is softened and the foul odor has gone;"
et aucune fois est clisterizeis d’aigue de cendres,	"Sometimes it is also poulticed with ash water;"
quant ceste medicine n’est presens, et est que tu preignes cendres de fust de vigne, et giete aigue desus,	"If this poultice is not available, then take some ashes from burnt grapewood and pour hot water over them;"
puis la coule, et en clisterize, tant que tu saiches que li seins est bien mondez;	"Then strain it and apply it as a poultice until you know that the boil has softened;"
et se li malaides ne le puet soffrir, ne la medicine egiptiaine ne l’aigue de cendres,	"If the patient cannot tolerate this treatment or if neither the Egyptian poultice nor ash water helps,"
si le clisterize d’aigue et de miel ou il ait un poc de litargire broiet;	"then apply a poultice of warm water and honey with a little crushed lead;"
ou tu la clistirize de miel et de vin melleit, que li mielz ait proprieteit de mundifiier et de laver,	"Or mix honey and wine that has the property to soften and wash away impurities,"
et li vins fait aerdre le sain;	"and let the wine cause the wound to scar;"
et quant tu as ce fait, et tu as fiance que li seins est bien mundifiiez,	And when you have done this, and you are confident that the breast is well cleansed,
si le clisterize de ceu que fait naistre char en li,	if the enema produces waste from within it,
et est que tu preignes emplaustre diafinit, et le font avec oile roset et en vin;	And you must take some dried powdered frankincense,
ou tu le clisterize d’aucunes medicines et d’oignemens, dont j’ai dit les proprietez ou traitier des oignemens;	Where you apply a clyster of certain medications and unguents, whose properties I have discussed in treating ointments;
et se li pertus dou sein est petis, et li cainne dou clistere n’i puet entrer,	and if the opening of the chest is small, and the tube of the clyster cannot enter;
si l’eslarge d’un fer un poc, et met ens une tente de l’oignement egiptiein,	If he widens a little with an iron tool, and places within it a cloth of Egyptian ointment.
ou oignement basilicon, tant k’il soit eslargiez;	or basilicon ointment, until it is widened sufficiently;
et se li plaie est trop large, si la cout et i laisse tant soulement .i. leu ou li clistere puisse entrer,	"And if the wound is too wide, then stitch it up and leave it just one space where the clyster can enter."
et se li pertus que giete bowe est au desus, si le cope ou plus bas leu que i est.	"And if the hole that shoots the bow is above, then cut off the tip or a little below where it is."
Car quant li bowe est en parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char;	"For when the bow is at full draw, no flesh should be allowed to enter [the bowstring]."
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues,	"And if you cannot cover the breast underneath as you see."
si appareille en tel maniere que li bowe corre au plus bas leu que i est,	"So it appears in such a way that the bow runs to the lowest point where it is."
car quant li bowe est parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char	Because when the bowel is perforated, no flesh remains within
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues,	and if you cannot cover the chest beneath it as you see,
si apareille en teil maniere: que li bowe corre legierement aval, et n’i lassier rien de la bowe;	**If prepared thus:**
et pren medicines consolidatives por mettre sor le sein,	"And take consolidative medicines to apply to the chest,"
et estent sus .i. drapeil de lin que cuevre tout le sein;	"And place a linen cloth on it that covers the entire chest;
puis cope as forces endroit le pertus dou sein .i. poc plus large dou premier,	Then strike with force against the heart's doorway, a little more than a finger's width.
pues estent oignement souef sus .i. autre drapel selonc la quantiteit dou pertus,	and then lay gently upon it another piece of cloth according to the size of the hole.
et le met sus le pertus dou sein por aligier la bowe, et n’oster mie le grant drapeil fuers que aprés maint jor une fois;	"And place it on the breast's opening to relieve the bow, but do not remove the large cloth outward until after many days once."
et celui qui est sor le pertus dou sein, oste sovent por oster la bowe,	"and whoever is over the breast's opening often pulls to relieve the bow,"
et saiches ceu que corra de la bowe, se c’est venin ou poc ou assez, ou digeste, ou indigeste;	"And know what comes from the bowels, whether it is venom or pus or enough, or digested or undigested;"
et pren warde se li patiens sent dolor ou nom, et s’il i a aposteme ou non,	"And take care if the patient feels pain or not, and if there is an abscess or not."
et quant ta medicine s’est en teil maniere estendue et tu vois la nature que saut sus le pertus dou sein,	"When that medicine has been applied in such a manner that you see it oozing out of the opening of the chest,"
si saiches que li seins s’aert ja, et aproche li santez;	"If you know that the chest is already inflamed, and the wound approaches the sound part (of the body);"
et puis le deslie le matin, ou le tier jor, et quant tu delies la plaie,	And then untie it in the morning or on the third day, once you have healed the wound.
si chainge .i. autre drapeil, et renovele l’oignement.	Then change one other bandage and renew the ointment.
Et se li seins giete bowe indigeste aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie.	And if the breast becomes painful and swollen after many days, know that the breast is not healed yet.
